\#\#\# EVA Transcription Notes for F76r

‚Äî R.34 ends with \`=\` marking a SECTION BOUNDARY. The specification divides into three major parts: R.1‚ÄìR.34 (the core rules), R.35‚ÄìR.47 (final verification rules).  
‚Äî Three \`p\!\!\!\` decorated headers: R.1 (opens specification), R.30 (opens verification section), R.35 (opens final rules).  
‚Äî One \`f\!\!\!\` atom at R.41 ‚Äî the Venus/growth principle RETURNS near the specification's close, bracketing the first two bath folios.  
‚Äî Station labels appear at R.4 (s), R.6 (d), R.8 (q), R.11 (s), R.14 (o), R.17 (l), R.21 (k), R.24 (k), R.29 (s).

\#\# 3\. THE NINE-STATION TEST NETWORK

The single-character labels define the MINIMUM VIABLE TEST SUITE ‚Äî the smallest set of tests that verifies a complete purification cycle:

| Position | Label | VML Prefix | Test Type | Frequency |  
|----------|-------|-----------|-----------|-----------|  
| R.4 | s | SALT | Crystallization test | √ó3 (most frequent) |  
| R.6 | d | FIX | Stabilization test | √ó1 |  
| R.8 | q | EXTRACT | Circulation test | √ó1 |  
| R.11 | s | SALT | Crystallization test (repeat) | ‚Äî |  
| R.14 | o | HEAT | Thermal activation test | √ó1 |  
| R.17 | l | LAYER | Stratification test | √ó1 |  
| R.21 | k | BODY/CONTAIN | Containment test | √ó2 |  
| R.24 | k | BODY/CONTAIN | Containment test (repeat) | ‚Äî |  
| R.29 | s | SALT | Crystallization test (third) | ‚Äî |

\*\*The network alphabet: s‚Äìd‚Äìq‚Äìs‚Äìo‚Äìl‚Äìk‚Äìk‚Äìs\*\*

Salt (s) appears THREE TIMES ‚Äî at beginning, middle, and end ‚Äî making crystallization the GOLD STANDARD of purity testing. Containment (k) appears TWICE ‚Äî body containment requires redundant verification. Fixation (d), extraction (q), heat (o), and layering (l) each appear ONCE ‚Äî tested definitively. Nine stations, six categories: this is the COMPLETE QUALITY CONTROL PROTOCOL.

\#\# 4\. CRITICAL RULE PARAGRAPHS ‚Äî VML TRANSLATION AND ANALYSIS

\#\#\# R.1: The Opening Specification

\`p\!\!\!otchokar.chcphdy.opshdy.qolp.chcphy.chcphdy.opshey.qofshy.opchdy.sain.asy\`

\*\*VML:\*\* PROJECT-TEMPORAL-VOLATILE-HEAT-ROOT (full operational chain invoked in first token) | THREE \`chcph-\` tokens \= conduit-projection-heat compound stated three times | THREE \`op-\` tokens \= expansion/projection stated three times | Closes with \`sain\` \= salt-COMPLETE.

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "PROJECT the full temporal-volatile-heat-root cycle. Channel-project-heat the volatile. Expand the projection. Circulate through layers. Channel-project-heat AGAIN. Expand the transition. Circulate through formative vigorous flow. Expand the volatile. Salt test PASSED."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The TRIPLE cph- and TRIPLE op- establish CONDUIT PHYSICS as central to the specification. The bath section governs CONDUITS ‚Äî the physical tubes, condensers, and channels through which material flows. The \`cph-\` morpheme is rare outside the bath section and may encode the specific alembic-condenser apparatus.

\#\#\# R.5: The Triple-E Salt Token ‚Äî Defining Maximum Purity

\`soleeedy.qokeedy.qopchedy.qokeey.kol.shedy.qokedy.sheey.okeer.al.al.chedainda\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`soleeedy\` \= SALT-FLUID-\*\*TRIPLE-E\*\*-FIXED ‚Äî TRIPLE-E intensity as a SALT PROPERTY | \`al.al\` \= structure-structure DOUBLED | \`chedainda\` \= volatile-DAIIN(verified)-fix

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Salt flowing at TRIPLE INTENSITY. Extract essence fixed. Transmute fluid volatile. Extract essence active. Contain in fluid. Settle. Extract fixed. Transition essence active. Phase essence energy. Structure DOUBLED. Volatile verified-and-fixed."

\*\*Significance:\*\* Where f75r P.37 demonstrated triple-E as an operational EVENT (qokeeedy ‚Äî something that HAPPENS during a climax), f76r R.5 DEFINES triple-E as a salt PROPERTY (soleeedy ‚Äî something that IS TRUE of pure salt). Triple-E is not just high intensity ‚Äî it is the SPECIFICATION OF PHARMACEUTICAL-GRADE PURITY. When salt crystallizes at triple-E concentration, the purification has reached its theoretical maximum. The doubled \`al.al\` (structure-structure) and the compound \`chedainda\` (volatile-verified-fixed) confirm that this token defines the END STATE of purification.

\#\#\# R.8: The Central Valve Specification ‚Äî The Master Interlock

\`qotedshedy.qorain.oteedy.chedy.ol.chdy.raiiin.chekain.dain.chckhy.sal.oty\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`raiiin\` \= rotation-\*\*TRIPLE-I\*\* (extended temporal cycling ‚Äî three times standard duration) | \`dain.chckhy.sal.oty\` \= CHECKPOINT ‚Üí CKH-VALVE ‚Üí SALT ‚Üí TEMPORAL-ACTIVE

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Transmute-heat-transition-settle. Transmute-rotation-complete. Temporal essence-energy fixed. Volatile fixed. Fluid. Channel fixed. Rotation through TRIPLE EXTENDED CYCLING. Volatile body complete. CHECKPOINT. VALVE. SALT TEST. Temporal active."

\*\*Significance:\*\* This is the CENTRAL INTERLOCK RULE ‚Äî the master sequence that must execute at every checkpoint: rotation ‚Üí verify ‚Üí valve ‚Üí salt ‚Üí time. The triple-I (\`raiiin\`) echoes the triple-I in astrological nymph labels (okaiiin) ‚Äî extended cycling operates identically across domains. The sequence \`dain.chckhy.sal.oty\` defines the four-element verification: checkpoint confirms readiness, valve confirms flow control, salt confirms purity, temporal activation confirms timing. ALL FOUR must pass.

\#\#\# R.13: The Embedded Triple-E ‚Äî Peak-Intensity Protocol

\`chey.chckh.sheoqeeey.chol.lkain.shedy.qokeedy.okain.chedy.okeed.qokaloro\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`sheoqeeey\` \= transition-heat-transmute-\*\*TRIPLE-E\*\*-active | \`chckh\` \= CKH valve in bare/specification mode | \`qokaloro\` \= extract-structure-fluid-rotation-heat (compound extraction pathway)

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Volatile active. VALVE \[specification mode\]. Transition at TRIPLE-E INTENSITY through heat-transmutation. Volatile heated fluid. Layer-contain-complete. Settle. Circulate. Phase complete. Volatile fixed. Phase essence energy. Extract through full structural-fluid-rotation-heat pathway."

\*\*Significance:\*\* This rule specifies what happens when the valve encounters peak-intensity material. The entire extraction pathway is encoded in a single compound token: \`qokaloro\` \= structure ‚Üí fluid ‚Üí rotation ‚Üí heat. Material passes through FOUR DOMAINS in sequence during peak extraction. The valve operating in bare \`chckh\` form (without suffix) indicates SPECIFICATION MODE ‚Äî defining the rule rather than executing it.

\#\#\# R.16: The Convergence Endpoint ‚Äî What "Done" Looks Like

\`qokchsdy.okeey.lchedy.qo.olain.ot.shedy.qotaly.dar.sain.shedy.oleeed\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`oleeed\` \= FLUID-\*\*TRIPLE-E\*\*-FIXED | \`dar.sain.shedy.oleeed\` \= fix-root ‚Üí salt-complete ‚Üí settle ‚Üí fluid-TRIPLE-E-fixed

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Extract volatile fixed. Phase essence active. Layer volatile fixed. Transmute. Fluid complete. Temporal. Settle. Transmute-heat-structure active. Fix at root. Salt COMPLETE. Settle. Fluid at TRIPLE-E concentration, FIXED."

\*\*Significance:\*\* This is the ENDPOINT SPECIFICATION ‚Äî the formal definition of PHARMACEUTICAL-GRADE PRODUCT. After fixation at root, after salt test passes, after settling, the fluid reaches triple-E concentration and is FIXED. The sequence \`dar.sain.shedy.oleeed\` is the FOUR-STEP CONCLUSION: fix, salt-confirm, settle, product-at-maximum. When you see \`oleeed\` in subsequent folios, it means the material has achieved this standard.

\#\#\# R.22: The Oscillation Ratio ‚Äî Patience Yields Purity

\`qokar.shedy.shedy.qokar.shedy.qokain.dar.shey.lshcthy.okar.okain.ydaiiny\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`qokar.shedy.shedy.qokar.shedy\` \= EXTRACT-SETTLE-SETTLE-EXTRACT-SETTLE (2 extractions, 3 settles) | \`ydaiiny\` \= moist-DAIIN(verified)-active

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Extract to root. Settle. Settle. Extract to root. Settle. Extraction COMPLETE. Fix at root. Transition active. Layer through conduit. Phase at root. Phase complete. VERIFIED and active."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The extraction-settle ratio is stated EXPLICITLY: 2:3. Two extractions per three settles. The system spends MORE TIME SETTLING THAN EXTRACTING. This is not inefficiency ‚Äî it is the fundamental principle of fractional separation. Most of the work in distillation happens during the WAITING: fractions separate by gravity, heavy components sink, light components rise, crystals form, oils float. The active extraction merely initiates the process; the passive settling completes it. In modern chromatography, the same principle applies: the column run takes minutes; the equilibration takes hours. Patience yields purity.

\#\#\# R.33: The Terminal Checkpoint ‚Äî Complexity Converges to Simplicity

\`dain.chey.lsh.daiin.chey\`

\*\*VML:\*\* dain \= CHECKPOINT | chey \= volatile-active | lsh \= layer-vigorous | daiin \= FULL VERIFICATION | chey \= volatile-active

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "CHECKPOINT. Volatile active. Layer vigorous. FULL VERIFICATION. Volatile active."

\*\*Significance:\*\* FIVE TOKENS ONLY ‚Äî the shortest rule in the entire specification. After 32 complex rules averaging 10-12 tokens each, the terminal checkpoint REDUCES to five. This mirrors the convergence algorithm itself: complexity reduces until the output is simple enough to state briefly. The specification's conclusion proves its own thesis ‚Äî when the system has converged, the description becomes minimal.

\#\#\# R.41: The F-Atom Return ‚Äî Venus Brackets the Network

\`f\!\!\!chedy.g.sal.dol.shdy.olkedy.qokaiin.otal.oory\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`f\!\!\!chedy\` \= FORMATIVE/VEGETATIVE with \`\!\!\!\` emphasis \= F-ATOM RETURNS | \`g\` \= \*\*GRADATIO\*\* (stepwise change ‚Äî rare morpheme from Scorpio f73r) | \`sal.dol\` \= salt \+ fix-fluid | \`otal\` \= temporal-structure (astrological scheduling morpheme)

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "GROWTH PRINCIPLE with gradual stepwise change: salt from fixed fluid, vigorous flow fixed, fluid body extracted through extended cycle, timed structure, heated rotation active."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The f-atom opened f75r P.1 (the network initializer) and now appears in f76r R.41 (near the specification's close). Venus's growth principle BRACKETS the first two bath folios: f75r opens with growth, f76r closes with growth. The \`g\` glyph (gradatio \= stepwise change) appeared in Scorpio (f73r S1.11) and now emerges in the bath specification ‚Äî growth occurs GRADUALLY through iterative purification. The \`otal\` morpheme bridges the Astronomical section's scheduling into the Bath section's rules: timing governs purification. This single paragraph weaves together THREE sections of the manuscript (Herbal growth, Astronomical timing, Bath purification) in nine tokens.

\#\#\# R.43: The Extraction Cascade Rule

\`olsheed.qokedy.qokeedy.qokedy.lkedy.lsheedy.okar.shedy.otain\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`qokedy.qokeedy.qokedy\` \= extract-single ‚Üí extract-DOUBLE ‚Üí extract-single (low-HIGH-low oscillation)

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Fluid transitioned. Extract at single intensity. Extract at DOUBLE intensity. Extract at single intensity. Layer body fixed. Layer transition fixed. Phase at root. Settle. Temporal COMPLETE."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The specification DEFINES the extraction cascade pattern: low ‚Üí HIGH ‚Üí low oscillation, converging to temporal completion. This is the RULE behind f75r P.37's operational cascade. Where f75r showed it happening, f76r specifies that it MUST happen this way. The damped oscillation is not a coincidence ‚Äî it is a PRESCRIBED TECHNIQUE.

\#\# 5\. PLAIN-LANGUAGE TRANSLATION ‚Äî WHAT F76R ACTUALLY SAYS

Reading f76r as the quality control specification for a pharmaceutical purification facility:

\*\*THE TEST NETWORK (Station labels):\*\*  
"Nine test stations organized into six categories. Test for salt crystallization at three points (beginning, middle, end). Test for fixation stability once. Test extraction efficiency once. Test thermal response once. Test layer stratification once. Test body containment twice. This is the minimum test suite ‚Äî you cannot certify purity without passing all nine stations."

\*\*THE CORE RULES (R.1‚ÄìR.34):\*\*  
"Rule 1: The full purification cycle runs temporal ‚Üí volatile ‚Üí heat ‚Üí root, through conduit apparatus tested three times. Rule 5: Maximum purity is defined as salt crystallizing at triple-E concentration. Rule 8: At every checkpoint, the master interlock fires: rotation ‚Üí verify ‚Üí valve ‚Üí salt ‚Üí time. Rule 13: When the valve encounters triple-E intensity material, extract through the full four-domain pathway. Rule 16: The product is DONE when fluid reaches triple-E concentration and is permanently fixed. Rule 22: Extraction and settling alternate at a 2:3 ratio ‚Äî more settling than extraction. Rule 33: The terminal checkpoint is five words: check, verify, done."

What this FEELS like: You're reading the quality manual for the apothecary's workshop. It hangs on the wall. Every apprentice memorizes it. Every batch is tested against these standards. The rules are not suggestions ‚Äî they are REQUIREMENTS. A batch that fails any station must be reprocessed or discarded. The manual exists because without it, each practitioner would invent their own standards, and consistency would be impossible.

\*\*THE FINAL RULES (R.35‚ÄìR.47):\*\*  
"Final verification protocol: vigorous valve check at structure. Extract through extended cycling. Phase essence fixed at every stage. Checkpoint at valve under extended conditions. Salt extended test with vigorous flow. Salt and fluid extended life-cycle confirmed. Growth principle with gradual stepwise change. Salt from fixed fluid. Extract through damped oscillation (low-high-low). Salt extended life-cycle through all channels. Fix at structure through extended circulation. Salt confirmed with heat doubled at structure. Phase extended life-cycle through fluid with vigorous flow. Product extracted to essence active with vigorous flow fixed."

What this FEELS like: The final examination. Every rule has been stated. Now the specification runs through the entire system ONE LAST TIME, confirming that every station, every valve, every salt test, every temporal cycle meets the standard. The f-atom at R.41 is the signature ‚Äî Venus, the growth principle, endorses the specification. The system is certified.

\#\# 6\. COMPARISON TO FIFTEENTH-CENTURY PHARMACEUTICAL STANDARDS

\*\*The Pharmacopoeia Tradition:\*\* F76r functions as a PHARMACOPOEIA MONOGRAPH ‚Äî a formal specification of quality standards for a pharmaceutical product. The earliest pharmacopoeias emerged in the Islamic Golden Age (the \*AqrƒÅbƒÅdhƒ´n\* of Sabur ibn Sahl, ninth century) and were adopted in European practice through translations into Latin. By the fifteenth century, cities like Florence (the \*Ricettario Fiorentino\*, 1498\) and Nuremberg (the \*Dispensatorium\*, 1546\) were publishing official pharmacopoeias that REQUIRED specific purity standards for all medicinal preparations. F76r predates these printed pharmacopoeias but encodes the same principle: formal, testable, reproducible quality standards.

\*\*The Salt Crystallization Test:\*\* The triple salt-station emphasis (s-s-s) mirrors the medieval apothecary's reliance on crystallization as the PRIMARY purity indicator. The \*Lumen Apothecariorum\* (ca. 1450\) describes testing dissolved substances by evaporation and crystal examination: pure substances yield regular, well-formed crystals; impure substances yield irregular or failed crystallization. F76r's triple salt testing ‚Äî at beginning, middle, and end ‚Äî ensures that purity is confirmed not just once but at three stages of the process.

\*\*The Interlock Principle:\*\* The central interlock sequence (rotation ‚Üí verify ‚Üí valve ‚Üí salt ‚Üí time) corresponds to what modern pharmaceutical manufacturing calls a "hold point" ‚Äî a mandatory verification step that must be completed and documented before the process can continue. The medieval equivalent was the master's inspection: the apprentice could not proceed to the next step until the master confirmed the previous step's quality. F76r codifies this inspection into a four-element sequence.

\*\*The Oscillation Ratio:\*\* The 2:3 extraction-to-settling ratio defined at R.22 is consistent with practical distillation experience documented across centuries. Bernard of Gordon's \*Lilium medicinae\* (1303) advises that distillate should be allowed to "rest" between redistillations for at least as long as the distillation itself took. The Voynich specification formalizes this practical wisdom into an explicit ratio.

\#\# 8\. WHAT F76R TEACHES ‚Äî THE SEVEN RULES

1\. \*\*PURITY IS A SALT PROPERTY\*\* (R.5): Triple-E salt crystallization \= pharmaceutical grade. The specification defines purity by what the SALT does, not what the practitioner thinks.

2\. \*\*THE CENTRAL INTERLOCK\*\* (R.8): Rotation ‚Üí verify ‚Üí valve ‚Üí salt ‚Üí time. This four-element sequence fires at every checkpoint. No exceptions.

3\. \*\*CONDUIT PHYSICS MATTERS\*\* (R.1): Triple cph- tokens \= the specification governs the PHYSICAL APPARATUS, not just the chemical process.

4\. \*\*THE ENDPOINT IS DEFINED\*\* (R.16): \`oleeed\` \= fluid at triple-E, fixed. When you achieve this, you are DONE.

5\. \*\*PATIENCE YIELDS PURITY\*\* (R.22): Extract:settle \= 2:3. The system settles more than it extracts.

6\. \*\*COMPLEXITY CONVERGES TO SIMPLICITY\*\* (R.33): The terminal checkpoint is five tokens. Rules simplify at the end because the system has converged.

7\. \*\*VENUS ENDORSES\*\* (R.41): The f-atom brackets the purification network with the growth principle, connected by gradatio (stepwise change) to the full timing system.

\# FOLIO F76V ‚Äî THE ENDURANCE RUN  
\# SUSTAINED CONVERGENCE UNDER CLAMP CONTROL  
\# ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê

\#\# 1\. COMPLETE IMAGE DESCRIPTION

Folio 76 verso presents a bath diagram with SUSTAINED CYCLING PATTERNS. Nymph figures occupy pools that appear to be undergoing extended processing ‚Äî the visual impression is of material in CONTINUOUS MOTION. The text contains the longest unbroken cycling sequences in the entire bath section, with clamp/valve tokens appearing at regular intervals like heartbeats marking a steady operational rhythm.

\*\*What distinguishes this page visually:\*\* The regularity. Where f75r's text showed dramatic escalation (building to the triple-E climax) and f76r's text showed dense specification (rules packed tightly), f76v's text shows STEADY, RHYTHMIC REPETITION. The cycling patterns are long and even. The valve checks are evenly spaced. The impression is not of a climax or a reference document but of a SUSTAINED OPERATION ‚Äî a machine running at steady state for an extended period.

\*\*What a fifteenth-century practitioner saw:\*\* The ENDURANCE TEST PROTOCOL. Before committing to a full production run, the prudent practitioner asks: can the system maintain convergence over many cycles? Will the valve seals hold? Will the salt crystals remain consistent? Will the temperature stay stable? F76v answers these questions by running the system through an extended test ‚Äî the pharmaceutical equivalent of a stress test.

\*\*What a fifteenth-century patient saw:\*\* The LONG SOAK instructions. Some therapeutic bath treatments required extended immersion ‚Äî hours rather than minutes ‚Äî for chronic conditions. The medieval physician prescribed duration as carefully as temperature and herbal additives. F76v specifies the endurance limits of the bathing protocol.

\#\#\# EVA Transcription Notes for F76v

‚Äî P.33 ends with \`=\` marking a SECTION BOUNDARY within the endurance run. P.33 also closes the FIRST ENDURANCE PHASE (sustained cycling to convergence).  
‚Äî P.41 ends with \`=\` marking the FOLIO TERMINAL.  
‚Äî Three \`p\!\!\!\` headers: P.1 (opens endurance run), P.16 (second phase), P.25 (third phase).  
‚Äî P.13 contains TWO triple-E tokens: \`okeeedy\` (phase triple-E) and \`oleeedy\` (fluid triple-E).  
‚Äî P.19 contains DOUBLED valve: \`checkhy.checkhy\` (endurance valve fatigue management).  
‚Äî P.20 contains \`loiiim\` \= TRIPLE-I (layer-heat-triple-extended-union).  
‚Äî P.27 contains \`chlaiiin\` \= channel-layer-TRIPLE-I-cycle (second triple-I).  
‚Äî P.31 contains TWO triple-I tokens: \`shekaiiin\` (body-triple-I) and \`shetsaiiin\` (temporal-salt-triple-I).  
‚Äî P.25 contains \`sofcham\` \= salt-heat-\*\*F-ATOM\*\*-channel-union (Venus in endurance context).

\#\# 3\. CRITICAL PARAGRAPHS ‚Äî VML TRANSLATION AND ANALYSIS

\#\#\# P.1: Opening the Endurance Run

\`p\!\!\!olarar.okor.opcheey.yteey.opchaly.lshedy.qofchdal.lkodal.opa.korolr\`

\*\*VML:\*\* PROJECT-fluid-root-root (doubled root \= deep anchoring) | okor \= phase-heat-rotation | opcheey \= expand-volatile-essence-active | yteey \= moist-energy-essence-active | opchaly \= expand-volatile-structure-active | lshedy \= layer-settle | \`qofchdal\` \= transmute-\*\*F-ATOM\*\*-volatile-fix-structure (Venus growth embedded in transmutation) | lkodal \= layer-body-heat-fix-structure | opa \= expand-projection | korolr \= body-rotation-fluid-rotation (doubled rotation)

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "PROJECT: deep-rooted fluid. Phase-heat-rotate. Expand volatile essence. Moist energy active. Expand volatile structure. Layer and settle. Transmute through GROWTH PRINCIPLE with volatile fixation. Layer-body-heat-fix-structure. Expand projection. Body rotates through fluid rotation."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The endurance run opens with the f-atom (Venus growth) embedded directly in the transmutation command (\`qofchdal\`). Growth is not separate from purification ‚Äî it IS purification. The doubled root (\`olarar\`) and doubled rotation (\`korolr\`) frame the paragraph: material is deeply rooted and thoroughly rotated. The endurance run begins at FULL DEPTH and FULL MOTION.

\#\#\# P.13: The Double Triple-E ‚Äî Both Phases at Maximum

\`saiin.sheedy.qol.sheedy.okeeedy.qoteedy.chedy.qotedy.oleeedy.qoteedy.lo\`

\*\*VML:\*\* saiin \= salt-extended-cycle | \`okeeedy\` \= phase-\*\*TRIPLE-E\*\*-fixed | \`oleeedy\` \= fluid-\*\*TRIPLE-E\*\*-fixed | TWO triple-E tokens in separate domains

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Salt extended test. Transition fixed. Circulate. Transition fixed. Phase at TRIPLE-E INTENSITY, fixed. Transmute-heat double-E. Volatile fixed. Transmute-heat. Fluid at TRIPLE-E INTENSITY, fixed. Transmute-heat double-E. Layer."

\*\*Significance:\*\* TWO TRIPLE-E TOKENS IN ONE PARAGRAPH ‚Äî the endurance run's first peak. The SOLID material (phase domain: \`okeeedy\`) and the LIQUID material (fluid domain: \`oleeedy\`) BOTH reach triple-E simultaneously. Convergence requires ALL fractions to achieve maximum intensity independently. In practical terms: the crystals must be pharmaceutical-grade AND the liquid must be pharmaceutical-grade AT THE SAME TIME. Partial convergence is not convergence.

\#\#\# P.14: Maximum Density ‚Äî Pure Action

\`qokeedy.qol.cheedy.otedy.cthedy.otedy.qoteedy.shcthedy.qoeekeedy.deedy\`

\*\*VML:\*\* SIX extraction/transmutation commands | \`qoeekeedy\` \= transmute-ENERGY-body-essence-energy-fixed (five-morpheme compound) | \`deedy\` \= fix-essence-energy-fixed (double-locked)

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Extract essence fixed. Circulate. Volatile fixed. Temporal fixed. Conduit-bind fixed. Temporal fixed. Transmute-heat double-E fixed. Vigorous conduit fixed. Transmute-ENERGY-body-essence-fixed. Fix essence-energy LOCKED."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The PEAK DENSITY paragraph ‚Äî maximum operational throughput. Every token is an active command; there are NO SETTLE PHASES. This is the endurance run at MAXIMUM VELOCITY ‚Äî all operators running simultaneously, no pauses. This occurs at mid-run when the system has warmed up to peak performance. The five-morpheme compound \`qoeekeedy\` is one of the longest operational tokens in the bath section.

\#\#\# P.19: Double Valve ‚Äî Endurance Safety

\`orar.sheey.otar.shedy.otedy.checkhey.olchedy.checkhy.checkhy.lky\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`checkhy.checkhy\` \= DOUBLED VALVE CHECK | orar \= heat-rotation-root | otar \= temporal-root

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Heat-rotation at root. Transition essence active. Temporal at root. Settle. Temporal fixed. Valve check on fluid volatile. VALVE CHECK. VALVE CHECK \[DOUBLED\]. Layer moist active."

\*\*Significance:\*\* After sustained high-intensity cycling, the system requires DOUBLE VALVE VERIFICATION. Single-valve checks suffice during normal operation; the endurance run demands double-checking because sustained high intensity may cause valve seal fatigue, gasket degradation, or thermal expansion of fittings. This is ENGINEERING PRUDENCE ‚Äî the same reason modern industrial processes require more frequent safety inspections during extended continuous operation.

\#\#\# P.20: Triple-I ‚Äî Extended Cycling at Maximum Duration

\`dol.sheetey.qokedy.ol.checkhy.lshedy.qokeedy.cheedy.qokeedy.shl.loiiim\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`loiiim\` \= layer-heat-\*\*TRIPLE-I\*\*-union ‚Äî TRIPLE EXTENDED CYCLING reaching union

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Fix fluid. Transition essence energy active. Extract fixed. Fluid. Valve check. Layer settle. Circulate. Volatile fixed. Circulate. Vigorous layer. Layer-heat-TRIPLE-EXTENDED-UNION."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The endurance run produces triple-I cycling: the material's temporal phase extends to THREE TIMES standard duration before reaching union. Triple-I appeared in f76r R.8 as \`raiiin\` (rotation-triple-I); now in f76v P.20 it is \`loiiim\` (layer-triple-I-union). The specification DEFINED triple-I; the endurance run ACHIEVES it. The material runs for triple duration through heat layering and reaches union ‚Äî a state where all components have been integrated. In practical terms: the distillation runs three times longer than standard, and the resulting fraction is fully homogenized.

\#\#\# P.25: Venus in the Endurance ‚Äî Growth Through Purification

\`p\!\!\!sheoldy.opalshedy.qokshedy.qokedy.dor.shey.opchedy.dal.sofcham\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`sofcham\` \= salt-heat-\*\*F-ATOM\*\*-channel-union | opalshedy \= expand-project-structure-settle

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "PROJECT: transition-fluid-fixed. Expand-project-structure settle. Extract transition fixed. Extract fixed. Fix rotation. Transition active. Expand volatile fixed. Fix structure. Salt-heat-VENUS-channel-UNION."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The f-atom (Venus growth) is embedded in a SALT-CHANNEL-UNION compound. Growth and purification are UNIFIED at the endurance stage. The material does not just get purer ‚Äî it gets MORE POTENT. This reflects the medieval alchemical principle that purification CONCENTRATES the "virtue" (active potency) of a substance. A triple-distilled herbal extract is not just cleaner than a single distillate ‚Äî it is MORE MEDICINALLY POWERFUL. F76v's integration of Venus into the endurance run confirms that extended cycling increases both purity AND potency.

\#\#\# P.27: The Convergence Declaration ‚Äî Four Conditions

\`daiin.shckhey.qokeedy.saiin.chek.ain.rain.o.kan.chlaiiin\`

\*\*VML:\*\* daiin \= FULL VERIFICATION | saiin \= salt-extended-PASSED | rain \= rotation-COMPLETE | \`chlaiiin\` \= channel-layer-TRIPLE-I-cycle

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "VERIFIED. Vigorous valve active. Circulation fixed. Salt extended test PASSED. Volatile complete. Rotation COMPLETE. Heat. Contained. Channel-layer TRIPLE EXTENDED CYCLE."

\*\*Significance:\*\* Convergence is declared when FOUR CONDITIONS are simultaneously met: (1) full verification passes (daiin), (2) salt extended test passes (saiin), (3) rotation completes (rain), and (4) triple-extended cycling achieves channel-layer integration (chlaiiin). ALL FOUR must be true. Any single failure means the endurance run must continue. This is a CONJUNCTION of criteria ‚Äî the logical AND of four independent tests.

\#\#\# P.31: Maximum Intensity ‚Äî Parallel Triple-I

\`sair.shekaiiin.shetsaiiin.shety.otey.okaiin.otedy.qotar.chedy\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`shekaiiin\` \= transition-body-\*\*TRIPLE-I\*\* | \`shetsaiiin\` \= transition-temporal-salt-\*\*TRIPLE-I\*\* | TWO triple-I tokens on DIFFERENT substrates

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Salt at root PASSED. Transition body-essence through TRIPLE EXTENDED CYCLING. Transition temporal-salt through TRIPLE EXTENDED CYCLING. Transition temporal active. Temporal essence active. Phase double-cycle. Temporal fixed. Transmute-heat root. Volatile fixed."

\*\*Significance:\*\* TWO SEPARATE SUBSTRATES pushed through triple-extended cycling simultaneously: body-essence (\`shekaiiin\`) and temporal-salt (\`shetsaiiin\`). This is PARALLEL ENDURANCE ‚Äî testing whether multiple material fractions can sustain extreme duration at the same time. The body fraction and the salt fraction must BOTH survive triple-I cycling independently. In practical terms: the organic extract AND the mineral fraction must both remain stable through three times normal processing duration. If either degrades, the endurance test fails.

\#\#\# P.33: The Terminal ‚Äî Maximum Complexity Reduces to Three Words

\`sain.otaiin.shckhedy=\`

\*\*VML:\*\* sain \= salt COMPLETE | otaiin \= temporal-double-life-cycle | shckhedy \= vigorous-flow-CKH-VALVE-fixed

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Salt PASSED. Temporal cycle COMPLETE. Vigorous valve FIXED."

\*\*Significance:\*\* THREE TOKENS ONLY. After 33 paragraphs of sustained high-intensity cycling ‚Äî including double triple-E, parallel triple-I, doubled valves, five-morpheme compound extractions ‚Äî the conclusion REDUCES to three declarations: purity confirmed (sain), timing complete (otaiin), flow control locked (shckhedy). Maximum complexity ‚Üí minimum statement. This mirrors f76r R.33's five-token terminal. Both the specification AND the endurance run converge to BREVITY. The medium IS the message: convergence produces simplicity.

\#\# 4\. PLAIN-LANGUAGE TRANSLATION ‚Äî WHAT F76V ACTUALLY SAYS

Reading f76v as an endurance test protocol for a pharmaceutical purification system:

\*\*PHASE 1 ‚Äî WARM-UP AND RAMP (P.1‚ÄìP.15):\*\*  
"Open the endurance run at full depth and full rotation with growth embedded in the transmutation. Intensify. Circulate. Reach DAIIN verification twice (P.3, P.4). Test salt, conduit, and temporal response. Continue sustained cycling. At P.13, BOTH PHASES reach triple-E simultaneously ‚Äî the solid fraction and the liquid fraction are both at pharmaceutical maximum. At P.14, run at MAXIMUM VELOCITY ‚Äî every operator active, no settle phases. At P.15, brief consolidation."

What this FEELS like: You've loaded the system and started it running. The first few cycles warm everything up. The temperature stabilizes. The flow rate equilibrates. Then you push harder ‚Äî more heat, longer cycles. At P.13, you take samples from both the solid residue and the liquid distillate. Both test at maximum purity. At P.14, the system is running at absolute peak throughput ‚Äî every burner lit, every valve open, every condenser active. You're watching for any sign of failure.

\*\*PHASE 2 ‚Äî SUSTAINED HIGH-INTENSITY (P.16‚ÄìP.24):\*\*  
"Second phase: project through expansion with transition-fix. Salt at root with extended transitions. Layer through valve-transmutation chains with DAIIN verification (P.18). At P.19, DOUBLE VALVE CHECK ‚Äî endurance safety. At P.20, achieve TRIPLE-I extended cycling ‚Äî material runs three times normal duration through heat-layer-union. Conduit-bind at temporal-fluid with CKH valve. Salt and temporal cycling through structure. At P.23, fix-volatile, circulate, extract fluid, double settle with salt extended test. Brief consolidation at P.24."

What this FEELS like: The system has been running for hours. You're watching the valves carefully ‚Äî at P.19, you check them TWICE because sustained heat and pressure can cause seals to degrade. At P.20, you've reached triple duration ‚Äî the material has been cycling three times longer than a standard batch. Everything still looks good. The crystals are still forming cleanly. The distillate is still clear.

\*\*PHASE 3 ‚Äî CONVERGENCE AND VERIFICATION (P.25‚ÄìP.33):\*\*  
"Third phase: expand through growth-purification unity ‚Äî Venus embedded in salt-channel-union. At P.27, CONVERGENCE DECLARED: full verification passed, salt extended test passed, rotation complete, triple-I cycling achieved through all channels. Continue testing: salt with transition, salt with extraction, salt through all channels. At P.31, PARALLEL TRIPLE-I ‚Äî body essence AND temporal salt through triple extended cycling simultaneously. At P.32, temporal complete, transmute-heat complete, extended double-life cycle through valve at temporal-fluid. AT P.33: 'Salt PASSED. Temporal complete. Valve fixed.' THREE WORDS. DONE."

What this FEELS like: You've been watching this system run for what feels like an eternity. Finally, at P.27, all four convergence criteria are met simultaneously. But you don't stop ‚Äî you keep testing. More salt tests. More valve checks. At P.31, you push BOTH the organic extract and the mineral fraction through triple-duration cycling at the same time. Both hold. At P.33, you write three words in your log: "Salt good. Time complete. Valves sealed." You can stop. The system passed.

\*\*POST-CONVERGENCE CONFIRMATION (P.34‚ÄìP.41):\*\*  
"After convergence: continued verification under post-stress conditions. Salt and temporal cycling through expansion. DAIIN with volatile-fluid phase transitions. Transmute-energy through layers with salt extended tests. Salt extended with volatile-settle and circulation. Salt with transition and extraction. Salt with circulation and fluid. Salt extended CONFIRMED FINAL."

What this FEELS like: The endurance test is over, but you run a few more cycles just to be sure. You check everything one more time. Everything holds. You note it in the log, seal the batch record, and move on.

\#\# 5\. COMPARISON TO FIFTEENTH-CENTURY PRACTICE

\*\*Endurance Testing in Medieval Pharmacy:\*\* The concept of running a process for extended duration to verify its stability is documented in the \*Summa perfectionis\* (attributed to Pseudo-Geber, late thirteenth century), which describes subjecting purified substances to prolonged heating to confirm that they do not degrade. If the substance remains unchanged after extended exposure, it is declared "fixed" ‚Äî incapable of reverting to a less pure state. F76v formalizes this practice into a complete endurance protocol with explicit convergence criteria.

\*\*Parallel Fraction Testing:\*\* The requirement that BOTH solid and liquid fractions must independently achieve maximum purity (P.13's double triple-E, P.31's parallel triple-I) reflects genuine pharmaceutical necessity. Many medieval medicines contained BOTH a crystalline component (mineral salts, dried herb residue) and a liquid component (tincture, distilled essence). Both components must be independently pure. Contamination of either renders the whole medicine unsafe.

\*\*Valve Fatigue:\*\* The doubled valve check at P.19 corresponds to a real engineering concern in glass and ceramic apparatus. Prolonged heating causes thermal expansion; repeated cycling causes material fatigue; acidic or alkaline distillates can corrode valve seats over time. The Voynich author's insertion of double-valve checks at the endurance stage shows awareness of these failure modes.

|---------|-------|-------------|

| qo- circulation commands | \*\*70\*\* | Sustained cycling |  
| chckhy/ckh valve checkpoints | \*\*18\*\* | Regular pulse (every \~2.3 paragraphs) |  
| shedy settle phases | \*\*20\*\* | Work‚Üîsettle oscillation |  
| daiin/saiin markers | \*\*9\*\* | Frequent verification |  
| p\!\!\! section headers | \*\*3\*\* | Three endurance phases |  
| Triple-E tokens | \*\*2\*\* | okeeedy \+ oleeedy ‚Äî both domains |  
| Triple-I tokens | \*\*4\*\* | loiiim, chlaiiin, shekaiiin, shetsaiiin ‚Äî \*\*HIGHEST DENSITY\*\* |  
| Double-valve check | \*\*1\*\* | checkhy.checkhy ‚Äî endurance safety |  
| F-atom connection | \*\*1\*\* | sofcham ‚Äî Venus in endurance |

\#\# 7\. WHAT F76V TEACHES ‚Äî THE SIX LESSONS

1\. \*\*BOTH PHASES MUST CONVERGE\*\* (P.13): Phase triple-E AND fluid triple-E simultaneously. Partial purity is not purity.

2\. \*\*PARALLEL ENDURANCE\*\* (P.31): Multiple substrates through triple-extended cycling ‚Äî solid and liquid tested independently.

3\. \*\*VALVE FATIGUE IS REAL\*\* (P.19): Double-valve checks during sustained operation ‚Äî equipment degrades under stress.

4\. \*\*GROWTH THROUGH PURIFICATION\*\* (P.25): Venus integrates with salt-channel at the endurance stage ‚Äî extended cycling increases POTENCY as well as purity.

5\. \*\*FOUR-CRITERIA CONVERGENCE\*\* (P.27): Verification \+ salt \+ rotation \+ triple-I must ALL pass simultaneously.

6\. \*\*TERMINAL BREVITY\*\* (P.33): Three tokens close the run. Complexity converges to simplicity. The medium is the message.

\#\# F75R ‚Üí F76V ARCHITECTURAL PROGRESSION ‚Äî FOUR FOLIOS, ONE SYSTEM

| Folio | Function | Question Answered | Teaching Method |  
|-------|----------|------------------|-----------------|  
| f75r | Network Initialization | HOW does the system work? | 46 paragraphs of operational protocol |  
| f75v | Scale-Up | HOW MUCH can it handle? | Two-scale hierarchy with safety measures |  
| f76r | Stability Specification | WHAT RULES govern it? | 47 rules with nine-station test network |  
| f76v | Endurance Testing | HOW LONG can it run? | 41 paragraphs of sustained cycling |

After four folios, the system's architecture (f75r), scalability (f75v), rules (f76r), and endurance limits (f76v) are ALL DEFINED. The remaining sixteen folios (f77r‚Äìf84v) are APPLICATIONS of this system to specific purification tasks.

\# ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê  
\# FOLIO F77R ‚Äî THE ROUTING CONTROLLER  
\# NAMED CHANNELS ‚Äî WHERE MATERIAL FLOWS  
\# ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê

\#\# 1\. COMPLETE IMAGE DESCRIPTION

Folio 77 recto presents a bath network with EXPLICITLY LABELED CHANNELS. Each pipe connection between pools bears a text label identifying it as a named route. Nymph figures at network nodes. The diagram functions as EXECUTABLE PLUMBING ‚Äî an addressable system where every conduit has a name and every junction has a function.

\*\*What distinguishes this page visually:\*\* The LABELS ON THE TUBES. Previous folios labeled POOLS (f75r), NODES (f75v), and STATIONS (f76r). F77r labels the CONNECTIONS BETWEEN them. Approximately six channel labels appear along the top-tube route keys, creating the active routing alphabet. The text blocks are protocol paragraphs defining what happens ALONG each named route.

\*\*Architectural position:\*\* F77r completes the five-folio system definition:

| Folio | Function | Question Answered |  
|-------|----------|-------------------|  
| f75r | Network Initialization | HOW does the system work? |  
| f75v | Scale-Up | HOW MUCH can it handle? |  
| f76r | Stability Specification | WHAT RULES govern it? |  
| f76v | Endurance Testing | HOW LONG can it run? |  
| \*\*f77r\*\* | \*\*Routing Controller\*\* | \*\*WHERE does material flow?\*\* |

After f77r, the system is FULLY DEFINED ‚Äî architecture, scale, rules, endurance, routing. Everything from f77v onward is APPLICATION.

\*\*What a fifteenth-century practitioner saw:\*\* The PLUMBING DIAGRAM. Every tube, every connector, every junction has a name. When the master says "route this batch through Channel K to Station S," the apprentice consults f77r to know exactly which physical tube that means. This is the conduit map of the workshop.

\*\*What a fifteenth-century patient saw:\*\* The BATHHOUSE FLOOR PLAN showing named passages between pools. "Enter through Door A, proceed to Pool B, exit through Channel C." Medieval bathhouses posted directional instructions; f77r is the manuscript version.

\#\#\# EVA Transcription Notes for F77r

‚Äî P.16 ends with \`=\` marking a SECTION BOUNDARY. Routes divide: P.1‚ÄìP.16 (primary route specification) and P.17‚ÄìP.40 (secondary routes \+ verification).  
‚Äî Two \`p\!\!\!\` headers: P.1 (opens routing), P.30 (opens verification routes).  
‚Äî P.1 opens with \`p\!\!\!aldarairal\` ‚Äî the LONGEST SINGLE TOKEN in the bath section (14 characters), encoding the entire circular routing path.  
‚Äî P.9 contains QUINTUPLE qo- (five extraction/transmutation commands) with saiin centered \= extraction cascade with embedded salt test.  
‚Äî P.11 contains QUINTUPLE qo- again ‚Äî pure extraction route with no fixation.  
‚Äî P.16 contains \`lfcheal\` ‚Äî the F-ATOM embedded in a route seal.  
‚Äî P.22 contains \`chckhey...saiin\` ‚Äî the valve-salt interlock from f76r now ROUTED to a specific channel.  
‚Äî P.25 contains \`qoteeedy\` (triple-E) AND \`iiin\` (triple-I) ‚Äî both extremes in one paragraph.  
‚Äî P.32 contains \`daiiin\` ‚Äî TRIPLE EXTENDED VERIFICATION, unique to this folio.  
‚Äî P.38 contains double-DAIIN brackets (daiin opens AND closes).  
‚Äî P.39-40 close with three salt tests \+ absolute minimum terminal (2 tokens).

\#\# 3\. CRITICAL PARAGRAPHS ‚Äî VML TRANSLATION AND ANALYSIS

\#\#\# P.1: The Opening Route Declaration ‚Äî The Longest Token

\`p\!\!\!aldarairal.qokol.chey.qopchedy.qopchedy.dylches.alkedy.laly\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`p\!\!\!aldarairal\` \= PROJECT-structure-fix-root-complete-rotation-structure ‚Äî 14 characters encoding the ENTIRE circular routing path in a single compound morpheme: structure ‚Üí fixed ‚Üí rooted ‚Üí complete ‚Üí rotated ‚Üí BACK TO structure | \`qopchedy.qopchedy\` \= DOUBLED transmute-fluid-volatile-fixed

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "DECLARE ROUTE: \[Structure ‚Üí Fix ‚Üí Root ‚Üí Complete ‚Üí Rotate ‚Üí Structure\]. Extract to fluid. Volatile active. Transmute-fluid-volatile-fixed TWICE. Fix volatile active. Structure-body fixed. Layer-structure active."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The route is a CYCLE ‚Äî it starts at structure and returns to structure. All purification routes are circular, just as all distillation is cyclic. The doubled \`qopchedy\` confirms the route is traversed TWICE per cycle. The 14-character opening token is the bath section's equivalent of a FUNCTION SIGNATURE in programming: a single compound name that describes everything the function does.

\#\#\# P.4: Dual-Channel Verification Route

\`solteedy.qoteedy.qodeedy.chedaiin.chedy.shedaiin.sheolol.ched\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`chedaiin\` \= volatile-DAIIN (volatile VERIFIED) | \`shedaiin\` \= transition-DAIIN (transition VERIFIED) | \`qoteedy.qodeedy\` \= transmute-heat-double-E \+ transmute-fix-double-E

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Salt-fluid energy fixed. Transmute-heat double-E. Transmute-fix double-E. Volatile VERIFIED. Volatile fixed. Transition VERIFIED. Transition fluid elevated. Volatile."

\*\*Significance:\*\* DUAL-CHANNEL VERIFICATION ‚Äî both the volatile product AND the transition process are independently verified before the route is cleared. The product must be pure AND the process must have run correctly. This is the pharmaceutical equivalent of batch record review: verify what you made AND verify how you made it.

\#\#\# P.9: The Quintuple QO Cascade

\`qoteedy.qoteedy.qokedy.sheed.qeey.saiin.sheety.qokeedy.lol\`

\*\*VML:\*\* FIVE qo- commands in one paragraph: qoteedy (√ó2), qokedy, qeey, qokeedy | saiin centered \= salt test EMBEDDED within the cascade | Closes with \`lol\` \= layered fluid output

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Transmute-heat double-E. Transmute-heat double-E. Extract fixed. Transition essence. \[Rare extract-essence active\]. Salt extended test. Transition active. Circulate. Layered fluid."

\*\*Significance:\*\* This route IS the extraction cascade ‚Äî five consecutive operations with a salt test at their geometric center. The route's output is \`lol\` (layered fluid) ‚Äî the standard output format for a converged batch where all fractions have separated into clean strata.

\#\#\# P.11: Pure Extraction Route ‚Äî Second Quintuple QO

\`qokeedy.lchey.lsheey.qokeedy.qokeedy.qokar.qokeey.laiin.chey\`

\*\*VML:\*\* FIVE qo- commands: qokeedy (√ó3), qokar, qokeey | NO fixation, NO settling, NO valves | \`laiin\` \= layer-double-life-cycle (extended layering)

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Extract essence fixed. Layer volatile active. Layer transition active. Extract essence fixed. Extract essence fixed. Extract to root. Extract essence active. Extended layer cycle. Volatile active."

\*\*Significance:\*\* A PURE EXTRACTION ROUTE ‚Äî nothing but extraction and layering. This route exists for material that has ALREADY been purified and just needs to be MOVED. No quality testing, no settling, no verification. Pure throughput. In a factory, this is the TRANSFER LINE between two process units ‚Äî it moves product, it doesn't transform product.

\#\#\# P.16: The Route Seal ‚Äî Venus in Infrastructure

\`daiin.dol.shar.cphey.lfcheal.shear.qolchy=\`

\*\*VML:\*\* daiin \= FULL VERIFICATION | dol \= fix-fluid | \`lfcheal\` \= layer-\*\*F-ATOM\*\*-volatile-structure ‚Äî Venus embedded in route seal | Ends with \`=\` \= SECTION BOUNDARY

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "VERIFIED. Fix fluid. Vigorous root. Conduit active. Layer GROWTH-volatile-structure. Transition root. Transmute-layer-volatile."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The f-atom appears at the point where a channel is OFFICIALLY CLOSED and its contents are committed. Venus governs not just the material but the INFRASTRUCTURE ‚Äî the channel itself carries the growth principle. The \`=\` boundary seals the primary routing section. After this point, routes are secondary (verification, extreme, terminal).

\#\#\# P.22: The Valve-Salt Interlock ‚Äî Rule Becomes Route

\`qokaiin.chckhey.saiin.qoklain.cheeky.lol\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`chckhey\` \= CKH VALVE | \`saiin\` \= salt extended test | VALVE ‚Üí SALT in direct sequence

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "Extract extended cycle. CKH VALVE CHECK. Salt extended test. Extract layer-complete. Volatile essence active. Layered fluid."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The valve-salt interlock from f76r's specification (R.8: rotation ‚Üí verify ‚Üí valve ‚Üí salt ‚Üí time) is now ROUTED ‚Äî assigned to a specific physical channel. The interlock is no longer an abstract rule; it is a PHYSICAL LOCATION in the network. When the practitioner needs to run a valve-salt check, they send material to THIS route.

\#\#\# P.25: The Extreme Route ‚Äî Triple-E Meets Triple-I

\`daiin.chedy.qolkeedy.qoteeedy.sar.iiin.cheety.dy\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`qoteeedy\` \= transmute-heat-\*\*TRIPLE-E\*\*-fixed | \`iiin\` \= \*\*TRIPLE-I\*\* (bare, unattached) | Both extremes in one paragraph

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "VERIFIED. Volatile fixed. Transmute-layer-body-essence fixed. Transmute-heat at TRIPLE-E INTENSITY, fixed. Salt at root. TRIPLE EXTENDED CYCLING. Volatile energy. Fixed."

\*\*Significance:\*\* Triple-E and triple-I appear TOGETHER for the first time in the bath section. The route passes through BOTH maximum intensity (triple-E) AND maximum duration (triple-I). This is the EXTREME ROUTE ‚Äî reserved for material requiring the highest possible purity at the longest possible processing time. In practice: the most precious or most dangerous substances that demand absolute pharmaceutical certainty.

\#\#\# P.32: Triple Extended Verification ‚Äî Unique to F77r

\`daiiin.ol.ee\*dy.okaiin.sheeol.qotaiin.shedy.qoty\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`daiiin\` \= fix-\*\*TRIPLE-I\*\* \= TRIPLE EXTENDED VERIFICATION ‚Äî the ONLY occurrence in the bath section | Where daiin \= full verification, daiiin \= EXTENDED full verification

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "TRIPLE-EXTENDED VERIFICATION. Fluid. \[Essence fixed ‚Äî damaged text\]. Phase double-cycle. Transition essence fluid. Transmute-heat double-cycle. Settle. Transmute-heat active."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The routing controller contains a route that requires TRIPLE VERIFICATION ‚Äî three times the standard verification duration. This route exists for the most critical products where any failure would be catastrophic. Three verification passes where one normally suffices. In modern terms: triple-checked quality for life-critical pharmaceuticals.

\#\#\# P.38: Double-DAIIN Brackets ‚Äî Verified Entering, Verified Exiting

\`daiin.chlchpsheey.tel.cheol.dad.yrotey.daiin\`

\*\*VML:\*\* \`daiin\` opens AND closes \= VERIFICATION BRACKETS | \`dad\` \= fix-structure-fix \= DOUBLED FIXATION in one compound

\*\*Plain language:\*\* "VERIFIED. Channel-layer-conduit-projection-transition active. Energy layer. Volatile fluid. DOUBLE-FIXED. Moist rotation heat energy. VERIFIED."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The route is BRACKETED by verification ‚Äî checked before entry, checked after exit. The \`dad\` compound (fix-ad \= fix-structure-fix) ensures material structure is locked TWICE during transit. Belt AND suspenders. Nothing passes through this route without being verified on both sides.

\#\#\# P.39-40: The Terminal Salt Cascade

\`ysheey.dal.saiiral.sal.dalo.tain.dary.dalo\` / \`sodar.oloky\`

\*\*VML:\*\* P.39: THREE salt tests (\`saiiral\`, \`sal\`, \`dalo\`) \+ doubled structural fixation under heat | P.40: TWO TOKENS ONLY ‚Äî \`sodar.oloky\` \= salt-fix-root \+ fluid-phase-active

\*\*Plain language:\*\* P.39: "Moist transition active. Fix structure. Salt-EXTENDED-rotation-structure. Salt test. Fix-structure-heat. Temporal complete. Fix-root active. Fix-structure-heat." P.40: "Salt-fixed-root. Fluid-phase active."

\*\*Significance:\*\* The routing controller ends like every bath folio: MAXIMUM BREVITY after maximum complexity. P.39 runs three salt tests with doubled fixation. P.40 closes with two words: salt-fixed, fluid-active. Forty paragraphs of intricate routing reduced to TWO TOKENS. The practitioner reads those two tokens and knows: "The system is clean. The product flows."

\#\# 4\. PLAIN-LANGUAGE TRANSLATION ‚Äî WHAT F77R ACTUALLY SAYS

Reading f77r as the conduit map for a pharmaceutical facility:

\*\*PRIMARY ROUTES (P.1‚ÄìP.16):\*\*  
"Route Declaration: All routes are CIRCULAR ‚Äî material returns to where it started, purified. The primary route runs structure ‚Üí fix ‚Üí root ‚Üí complete ‚Üí rotate ‚Üí structure, traversed TWICE per cycle. Sub-routes handle salt verification (P.2), dual-channel verification (P.4), extraction cascades (P.9, P.11), heat transmutation (P.12), and verified completion (P.13). Each sub-route ends at a known state. Route P.16 SEALS the primary routes with Venus's growth principle embedded in the channel ‚Äî the infrastructure itself participates in growth."

\*\*SECONDARY AND VERIFICATION ROUTES (P.17‚ÄìP.29):\*\*  
"After the primary routes are sealed: secondary routes handle temporal fixed extraction (P.17), triple-transmutation cascades (P.18), salt-fluid completion (P.19), vessel delivery (P.20 ‚Äî \`lam\`), extended salt testing (P.21), the valve-salt interlock assigned to a physical channel (P.22), the extreme route at triple-E and triple-I (P.25), extended-cycle extraction with verification (P.26-27), and structural fixation with fluid output (P.28-29)."

\*\*TERMINAL ROUTES (P.30‚ÄìP.40):\*\*  
"Verification-phase routes opened by second p\!\!\! header. Triple extended verification (P.32 ‚Äî daiiin). Full rotation with completion (P.33 ‚Äî rain). Quadruple extraction cascade (P.34). Rotation-extended heat transmutation (P.35). Fluid transmutation output (P.36). Salt-channel-rotation (P.37). Double-bracketed verification (P.38 ‚Äî daiin...daiin). Terminal salt cascade ‚Äî three tests (P.39). Terminal: salt-fixed, fluid-active (P.40 ‚Äî two tokens)."

What this FEELS like: You're reading the workshop's conduit manual. Every tube, every connector, every named passage is listed with its specification. When something needs to flow from HERE to THERE, you look up the route and follow it. The manual is EXHAUSTIVE ‚Äî forty routes covering every possible material path through the facility. And it ends with two words: clean. flowing.

\#\# 5\. COMPARISON TO FIFTEENTH-CENTURY PRACTICE

\*\*Named Conduits in Medieval Workshops:\*\* The practice of naming laboratory apparatus and connections is documented in monastic and apothecary records. Benedictine scriptoria labeled their ink-making vessels; apothecary workshops named their distillation trains. The \*Mappae Clavicula\* (twelfth-century compilation) describes a workshop layout where each piece of apparatus has a specific designation. F77r formalizes this naming practice into a complete routing system.

\*\*Circular Routes:\*\* The circular routing principle (material returns to its starting point, purified) corresponds exactly to the practice of REDISTILLATION or COHOBATION ‚Äî collecting the distillate and running it through the same apparatus again. Each pass increases purity. F77r's double-traversal of the primary route (\`qopchedy.qopchedy\`) specifies exactly two redistillation passes through the same conduit.

\*\*The Extreme Route:\*\* The co-occurrence of triple-E (maximum intensity) and triple-I (maximum duration) in P.25 corresponds to the preparation of the most potent pharmaceutical compounds, such as \*aurum potabile\* (drinkable gold) or concentrated herbal quintessences, which required both extreme concentration AND extended processing time.

|---------|-------|-------------|  
| Total paragraphs | \*\*40\*\* | Full routing protocol |  
| qo- circulation commands | \*\*111\*\* | \*\*HIGHEST QO- COUNT\*\* in bath section |  
| chckhy/ckh valve checkpoints | \*\*6\*\* | Lower than f76r (routes not rules) |  
| shedy settle phases | \*\*16\*\* | Moderate oscillation |  
| daiin verification markers | \*\*11\*\* | \*\*HIGHEST DAIIN COUNT\*\* ‚Äî every route verified |  
| sal/sar salt references | \*\*2+\*\* | Route-integrated salt testing |  
| p\!\!\! section headers | \*\*2\*\* | P.1 (primary routes), P.30 (verification routes) |  
| Triple-E token | \*\*1\*\* | qoteeedy (extreme route) |  
| Triple-I tokens | \*\*2\*\* | iiin (bare, P.25) \+ daiiin (triple verification, P.32) |  
| F-atom in route | \*\*1\*\* | lfcheal (Venus in channel seal, P.16) |  
| Quintuple-qo paragraphs | \*\*2\*\* | P.9, P.11 (maximum extraction density) |  
| Double-daiin brackets | \*\*1\*\* | P.38 (entry \+ exit verification) |  
| Longest single token | \*\*14 chars\*\* | p\!\!\!aldarairal (full circular route) |

\#\# 7\. WHAT F77R TEACHES ‚Äî THE SEVEN ROUTES

1\. \*\*ALL ROUTES ARE CIRCULAR\*\* (P.1): Material returns to structure after purification. Redistillation is the fundamental operation.

2\. \*\*DUAL-CHANNEL VERIFICATION\*\* (P.4): Verify the PRODUCT and the PROCESS independently.

3\. \*\*PURE THROUGHPUT ROUTES EXIST\*\* (P.11): Some routes only MOVE material, they don't transform it.

4\. \*\*VENUS SEALS THE INFRASTRUCTURE\*\* (P.16): The growth principle is embedded in the channel itself, not just the material.

5\. \*\*EXTREME ROUTES FOR EXTREME PRODUCTS\*\* (P.25): Triple-E \+ triple-I for the most precious substances.

6\. \*\*TRIPLE VERIFICATION FOR CRITICAL PRODUCTS\*\* (P.32): daiiin ‚Äî three passes where one normally suffices.

7\. \*\*MAXIMUM COMPLEXITY ‚Üí MINIMUM TERMINAL\*\* (P.39-40): Forty routes reduce to two words: salt-fixed, fluid-active.

\# FOLIO F77V ‚Äî THE FULL STATE MACHINE  
\# COMPLETE LIFECYCLE ‚Äî PORT NAMING THROUGH FINAL SEAL  
\# ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê

\#\# 1\. COMPLETE IMAGE DESCRIPTION

Folio 77 verso presents the most PROCEDURALLY COMPLETE bath page in the manuscript. The layout has two distinct zones: seven pool/node labels at the top (the PORT DECLARATION), followed by 37 protocol paragraphs organized into three processing phases. Nymph figures at nodes throughout. The visual impression is of a COMPLETE MACHINE ‚Äî initialization through oscillation through commitment through seal.

\*\*What distinguishes this page:\*\* It is the first folio that shows an ENTIRE purification run from start to finish. Where previous folios defined individual COMPONENTS ‚Äî the network (f75r), the scale (f75v), the rules (f76r), the endurance (f76v), the routes (f77r) ‚Äî f77v ASSEMBLES all of these into a single working machine. Every element from the previous five folios appears here in operational context.

\*\*What a fifteenth-century practitioner saw:\*\* The MASTER PROCEDURE. The complete instructions for running one batch from raw input to sealed product. This is the page you read the night before your first solo batch. This is the page the master tests the apprentice on before granting journeyman status.

\*\*What a fifteenth-century patient saw:\*\* The COMPLETE BATH REGIMEN from arrival to departure. Enter through Port 1, proceed through the seven stations, undergo the prescribed soaking and movement sequence, exit purified.

\#\#\# EVA Transcription Notes for F77v

‚Äî Seven port labels (L.1‚ÄìL.7) each terminated with \`=\` (boundary marker).  
‚Äî 37 protocol paragraphs ‚Äî COMPLETE LIFECYCLE from initialization through final seal.  
‚Äî P.3 contains BOTH \`keeey\` (body-TRIPLE-E) AND \`taiiin\` (temporal-TRIPLE-I) ‚Äî maximum intensity at maximum duration.  
‚Äî P.3 also contains \`ssheedy\` ‚Äî rare INTENSIFIED transition (doubled initial consonant).  
‚Äî P.5 contains \`checkhy.sal.shedy\` ‚Äî the f76r-specified INTERLOCK SEQUENCE in operational context.  
‚Äî P.7 closes with \`lam\` (layer-vessel) ‚Äî COMMIT POINT \#1.  
‚Äî P.9 contains THREE rare qe- tokens: qeedy, qeedeey, qedy ‚Äî ENERGY TRANSMUTATION CASCADE.  
‚Äî P.10 is THREE TOKENS ONLY ‚Äî breathing space between phases.  
‚Äî P.14 contains \`chalaiiin\` ‚Äî channel-structure-TRIPLE-I (maximum reflux path).  
‚Äî P.16 contains \`fchor\` ‚Äî F-ATOM-channel-source (Venus shapes the conduit).  
‚Äî P.19 contains DOUBLE DAIIN ‚Äî bracketed verification.  
‚Äî P.20 contains bare \`aiiin\` ‚Äî pure TRIPLE-I duration.  
‚Äî P.22 contains \`fchedy\` (F-ATOM volatile) \+ \`sain\` \+ double \`qokain\` ‚Äî Venus at commitment.  
‚Äî P.28 contains \`rain\` ‚Äî ROTATION COMPLETE (centrifuge stops).  
‚Äî P.30 contains doubled \`qokain.qokain\` ‚Äî double-confirmed extraction complete.  
‚Äî P.32 contains \`sarolsheedy\` ‚Äî 12-character macro command.  
‚Äî P.34 contains \`sockhey\` ‚Äî salt \+ CKH valve MERGED into one token.  
‚Äî P.35 contains \`qokam\` ‚Äî extract to VESSEL (terminal operation).  
‚Äî P.37 closes with \`okol\` ‚Äî phase-shift to FLUID (distillation complete).

\#\# 3\. THE SEVEN PORTS ‚Äî STATE MACHINE INPUT/OUTPUT

| Port | Label | Decode | Function |  
|------|-------|--------|----------|  
| L.1 | okain.akol | Phase-complete structured fluid | \*\*ENTRY\*\* ‚Äî pre-processed input |  
| L.2 | olkchdal | Trapped volatile in structural fluid | \*\*CONTAINMENT\*\* ‚Äî volatile locked |  
| L.3 | orchedal | Heat-rotation volatile extraction | \*\*DISTILLATION\*\* ‚Äî active separation |  
| L.4 | otol.shedy | Timed fluid settling | \*\*INPUT\*\* ‚Äî timer-controlled settling |  
| L.5 | otolor | Timed fluid projection | \*\*OUTPUT\*\* ‚Äî timer-controlled exit |  
| L.6 | sororal | Active salt crystallization test | \*\*QUALITY TEST\*\* ‚Äî dynamic salt |  
| L.7 | oleoedin | Reflexive essence cycling | \*\*SELF-PURIFICATION\*\* ‚Äî essence acts on itself |

\*\*Seven ports for seven functions:\*\* entry, containment, distillation, input, output, testing, self-purification. The complete lifecycle is addressable by port name. L.4 and L.5 form an INPUT/OUTPUT PAIR ‚Äî both timer-controlled, one receiving (shedy \= settling), one projecting (or \= source/projection). L.6 is DYNAMIC salt testing ‚Äî the test is active (flowing, rotating), not passive (sitting in a dish). L.7 is REFLEXIVE ‚Äî the essence purifies itself through cyclic self-action.

\#\# 4\. THE THREE PHASES ‚Äî FULL LIFECYCLE ANALYSIS

\#\#\# PHASE 1: INITIALIZATION (P.1‚ÄìP.9)

\*\*P.1 ‚Äî Cautious Startup:\*\* The state machine begins with a rare \`qe-\` prefix (energy-transmutation), then DOUBLED heat transmutation (\`qotedy.qotedy\`) before extracting. The first cycle applies heat TWICE before extracting ONCE and locks the result in structure (\`dal\`). Cautious initialization: double treatment, single extraction, structural lock.

\*\*P.2 ‚Äî Layered Circulation:\*\* Shifts to stratified settling. \`lshedy\` and \`qolsheedy\` \= the settling is now LAYERED. Material separates into strata. The rare \`qyrchs\` token may encode a specific apparatus configuration. Moisture (\`ydeedy\`) aids separation. Closes with reflux (\`qolky\`).

\*\*P.3 ‚Äî PEAK OPERATION:\*\* The state machine's most intense paragraph. \`keeey\` (body-TRIPLE-E) and \`taiiin\` (temporal-TRIPLE-I) together ‚Äî maximum intensity at maximum duration. The \`ssheedy\` (intensified transition, rare ss- prefix) shows INTENSIFIED settling. This is where the machine does its HARDEST WORK. After this paragraph, intensity diminishes as the system converges.

\*\*P.4 ‚Äî Condensation:\*\* The volatile BECOMES fluid ‚Äî \`cheol\` (volatile ‚Üí fluid) \= LITERAL CONDENSATION. Triple \`ol-\` tokens confirm the material is now predominantly liquid. Salt precipitates simultaneously (\`kshey\` \= body-salt). Two phase changes in one operation.

\*\*P.5 ‚Äî First Quality Gate:\*\* \`checkhy.sal.shedy\` \= VALVE ‚Üí SALT ‚Üí SETTLE. The f76r-specified INTERLOCK SEQUENCE in operational context. If all three pass, extraction continues. If any fails, the machine loops back. Closes with \`lol\` (layered fluid) \= standard converged output.

\*\*P.6 ‚Äî Valve as Processing Stage:\*\* \`qockhy\` opens \= circulating THROUGH the valve, not just checking it. The valve modifies material during passage. Closes with \`olchy\` (fluid volatile active) \= process NOT done, volatiles remain.

\*\*P.7 ‚Äî COMMIT POINT \#1:\*\* Closes with \`lam\` (layer-vessel) ‚Äî material is committed to a physical CONTAINER. After seven paragraphs of cycling, the first batch is locked in a vessel. \`am\` \= union/vessel.

\*\*P.8 ‚Äî Post-Commit Verification:\*\* After committing, the machine does NOT stop ‚Äî it introduces fresh salt solution (\`sor\`) to test the committed batch. 12 tokens \= the longest paragraph so far, reflecting additional verification steps post-commit.

\*\*P.9 ‚Äî Energy Transmutation Cascade:\*\* THREE rare qe- tokens (qeedy, qeedeey, qedy) in one paragraph ‚Äî the rarest prefix cluster in the bath section. This is ENERGY-LEVEL transmutation, deeper than physical separation. The 7-character \`qeedeey\` may be the most morphologically complex single token in the bath section. Closes with \`rar.ar\` (rotation-root \+ root) \= doubled root \= return to ground state after energy work.

\#\#\# PHASE 2: OSCILLATION AND CONVERGENCE (P.10‚ÄìP.28)

\*\*P.10 ‚Äî Breathing Space:\*\* THREE TOKENS ONLY (\`qol.kaiin.shey\`). After the energy cascade, the machine PAUSES. Material sits in its container for an extended period (\`kaiin\`), doing nothing but existing. Patience.

\*\*P.11 ‚Äî COMMIT POINT \#2:\*\* \`daiin...qokain\` \= VERIFIED \+ extraction COMPLETE. First extraction cycle declared done. But \`dary\` (fix-root-active) means the root is still active ‚Äî preparation for the next cycle begins immediately.

\*\*P.12 ‚Äî Convergence Indicator:\*\* Second daiin in two paragraphs. Closes with \`olol\` (doubled fluid) ‚Äî PURE FLUID, all solids removed. Same token appeared in f75v L2.3 as the reservoir label. The state machine has produced pure fluid.

\*\*P.13 ‚Äî Dynamic Fixation:\*\* \`dal.daly\` (fix-structure \+ fix-structure-ACTIVE) ‚Äî the structure is locked but contents remain energized. A sealed vessel with active liquid inside.

\*\*P.14 ‚Äî Maximum Reflux:\*\* \`chalaiiin\` \= channel-structure-TRIPLE-I. Material flows through a conduit for TRIPLE the standard duration. In distillation: a long reflux column. The longer the column, the better the separation.

\*\*P.15 ‚Äî Third Verification \+ Salt Test:\*\* \`daiin.sal\` \= VERIFICATION \+ SALT in direct sequence. Third daiin in five paragraphs. Machine health first (\`daiin\`), product quality second (\`sal\`).

\*\*P.16 ‚Äî Venus Shapes the Conduit:\*\* \`fchor\` \= FORMATIVE-channel-heat-rotation. The f-atom governs the channel through which heated rotating material flows. Growth (Venus) literally shapes the PHYSICAL CONDUIT. The 9-character \`qotasolky\` encodes a unified operation incorporating structure, salt, fluid, body simultaneously.

\*\*P.17 ‚Äî Heated Forced Completion:\*\* \`oqokain\` \= heat \+ extract-complete: extraction DRIVEN to completion by heat rather than allowed to finish naturally. Valve check (\`chckhy\`) verifies the forced completion was valid.

\*\*P.18 ‚Äî Salting and Spinning:\*\* Two salt-volatile compounds (\`chees\`, \`ches\`) in one paragraph. \`doraiin\` \= fix-source through extended rotation. CENTRIFUGAL SEPARATION with salting agents.

\*\*P.19 ‚Äî Bracketed Verification:\*\* DOUBLE DAIIN ‚Äî \`daiin...daiin\` \= verify BEFORE and AFTER the extraction. Followed by doubled \`qokedy.qokedy\` \= double-verified, double-extracted. Maximum confidence, maximum throughput.

\*\*P.20 ‚Äî Pure Duration:\*\* Bare \`aiiin\` (triple-I without prefix) \= the material simply CYCLES for triple standard time. No process applied, just TIME. After sufficient time: vigorous flow, extended extraction, salt test. Time as purification agent.

\*\*P.21 ‚Äî Fraction Separation:\*\* Valve (\`chckhy\`) falls BETWEEN stable extraction (\`qokedy\`) and volatile extraction (\`qokchy\`) ‚Äî the valve physically SEPARATES fractions. It is a FRACTION SEPARATOR, not just a checkpoint.

\*\*P.22 ‚Äî Venus at Commitment:\*\* \`fchedy\` (F-ATOM volatile fixed) appears between two \`qokain\` (extraction COMPLETE) markers, after \`sain\` (salt PASSED). Venus governs the MOMENT OF TRANSITION from process to product. The growth principle says: "This is ready."

\*\*P.23 ‚Äî Post-Gate Cleanup:\*\* Five tokens. Brief. After double-completion, just move the moist volatile into fluid channels. No verification needed ‚Äî past the quality gate.

\*\*P.24 ‚Äî Triple Fixation:\*\* \`daly.dal.dsheedy\` \= THREE consecutive fix operations. LOCKING DOWN after the quality gate. Material injection into hot liquid (\`pcheol\`), with formative/vegetative influence (\`lfol\`).

\*\*P.25 ‚Äî COMMIT POINT \#3:\*\* \`dal.daiin\` \= fix structure \+ FULL VERIFICATION. Third major verification. The control law in action: circulate, clamp, check, commit.

\*\*P.26 ‚Äî Worm Condenser:\*\* \`rchr\` (rotation-channel-rotation) \= DOUBLE ROTATION through a channel. Material rotates entering AND while inside. Helical flow through a tube ‚Äî the physical description of a WORM CONDENSER in a distillation apparatus.

\*\*P.27 ‚Äî Compound Extraction:\*\* \`qokalchedy\` \= FOUR-COMPONENT extraction (extract \+ structure \+ volatile \+ fixed) in a single token. Compound token \= compound operation. Valve checks before final structural extraction.

\*\*P.28 ‚Äî ROTATION COMPLETE:\*\* \`rain\` \= the centrifuge stops. All material separable by rotation HAS BEEN separated. \`sar\` (salt-at-root) tests the heaviest fraction. If salt passes at root, the entire batch is pure. The machine decelerates.

\#\#\# PHASE 3: COMMITMENT AND SEAL (P.29‚ÄìP.37)

\*\*P.29 ‚Äî Post-Rotation Fixation:\*\* \`dy.dy\` \= DOUBLED bare fixation. Simplest possible doubling ‚Äî "fix, fix." After rotation stops, material must be LOCKED before it re-separates.

\*\*P.30 ‚Äî Double-Confirmed Complete:\*\* \`qokain.qokain\` \= extraction complete TWICE. Doubled confirmation: "Is extraction complete?" "YES." "Are you SURE?" "YES."

\*\*P.31 ‚Äî Extended Salt Test:\*\* Five qo- commands with \`saiin\` (salt extended test). High extraction density before endurance salt verification.

\*\*P.32 ‚Äî COMMIT POINT \#4:\*\* \`sarolsheedy\` \= 12-character MACRO COMMAND encoding an entire sub-procedure. \`qokain...raiin...daiin\` \= extraction complete ‚Üí rotation extended ‚Üí FULL VERIFICATION. The final product is committed.

\*\*P.33 ‚Äî Post-Commit Byproduct Processing:\*\* After COMMIT POINT \#4, the machine keeps processing residual material. \`dolcheedy\` and \`solchedy\` handle byproducts.

\*\*P.34 ‚Äî Salt-Valve Fusion:\*\* \`sockhey\` \= salt \+ CKH valve MERGED into one token. Salt test and valve check SIMULTANEOUS. \`qokal.qokal\` \= doubled structural extraction from two fractions.

\*\*P.35 ‚Äî TERMINAL OPERATION:\*\* \`qokam\` \= extract to VESSEL. The \`-am\` suffix delivers product to its FINAL CONTAINER. \`saiin\` (extended salt test) confirms purity one last time before delivery.

\*\*P.36 ‚Äî Inline Verification:\*\* \`chdain\` \= channel-CHECKPOINT. The channel ITSELF contains a verification point ‚Äî material tested during transit, not before or after. \`ldche\*\` has manuscript damage (unreadable glyph).

\*\*P.37 ‚Äî DISTILLATION COMPLETE:\*\* Six tokens. Final \`okol\` \= phase-shift to FLUID. Everything that entered as solid exits as liquid. The state machine's output is a PHASE-SHIFTED FLUID. Distillation is done.

\#\# 5\. FOUR COMMIT POINTS ‚Äî STAGED PRODUCT DELIVERY

| \# | Paragraph | Marker | What's Committed |  
|---|-----------|--------|-----------------|  
| 1 | P.7 | \`lam\` (layer-to-vessel) | First batch to container |  
| 2 | P.11 | \`daiin...qokain\` (verified \+ complete) | First extraction cycle |  
| 3 | P.25 | \`dal.daiin\` (fix \+ verify) | Structure locked |  
| 4 | P.32 | \`qokain...raiin...daiin\` (complete \+ rotated \+ verified) | Final product |

Material is committed INCREMENTALLY through four staged checkpoints, not all at once. Each commit requires verification. The progression: container ‚Üí cycle ‚Üí structure ‚Üí product. Every stage must pass before the next commit.

\#\# 6\. COMPARISON TO FIFTEENTH-CENTURY PRACTICE

\*\*The Complete Batch Record:\*\* F77v functions as a complete BATCH RECORD ‚Äî the documented history of a single production run from charging the vessel to sealing the product. Medieval apothecary guilds increasingly required written records of production procedures, and the \*Ricettario Fiorentino\* (1498) formalized the requirement for documented manufacturing steps. F77v predates this formalization but encodes the same principle: every step, every test, every commitment point, documented.

\*\*Named Ports and Physical Apparatus:\*\* The seven named ports correspond to physically distinct pieces of apparatus: entry funnel (L.1), sealed vessel (L.2), alembic head (L.3), settling flask (L.4), delivery spout (L.5), crystallization dish (L.6), reflux loop (L.7). Each port name describes the physical configuration of that apparatus piece in VML morphemes.

\*\*The Worm Condenser:\*\* P.26's \`rchr\` (double rotation through channel) describes a SERPENTINE or WORM condenser ‚Äî a coiled tube through which vapor passes, condensing as it travels. The worm condenser was the signature innovation of fifteenth-century distillation, replacing the simpler straight-tube condenser with a coiled tube that vastly increased condensing surface area. Its description in VML confirms the manuscript's familiarity with state-of-the-art distillation apparatus.

\*\*Energy Transmutation:\*\* P.9's cluster of rare qe- tokens (energy transmutation) corresponds to the alchemical concept of \*transmutatio\* at the most fundamental level ‚Äî not merely separating physical components but transforming the material's essential NATURE. The \*Summa perfectionis\* distinguishes between \*separatio\* (physical separation) and \*transmutatio\* (essential transformation), placing the latter as the highest operation.

\#\# 8\. WHAT F77V TEACHES ‚Äî THE EIGHT LESSONS

1\. \*\*SEVEN PORTS COVER THE COMPLETE LIFECYCLE\*\* (L.1‚ÄìL.7): Entry, containment, distillation, settling, output, testing, self-purification ‚Äî every function has a named, addressable location.

2\. \*\*MAXIMUM INTENSITY AT MAXIMUM DURATION\*\* (P.3): Body-triple-E \+ temporal-triple-I together \= the peak operation. After this, the system only converges.

3\. \*\*ENERGY TRANSMUTATION GOES DEEPER THAN SEPARATION\*\* (P.9): Three qe- tokens \= the machine transforms the material's essential nature, not just its physical composition.

4\. \*\*FOUR STAGED COMMITS\*\* (P.7, P.11, P.25, P.32): Material is committed incrementally. Every commit requires verification. No single all-or-nothing release.

5\. \*\*BRACKETED VERIFICATION\*\* (P.19): Verify BEFORE and AFTER critical operations. Double daiin \= maximum confidence.

6\. \*\*VENUS GOVERNS COMMITMENT\*\* (P.22): The f-atom appears at the transition from process to product. Growth says "this is ready."

7\. \*\*INLINE VERIFICATION\*\* (P.36): Test DURING transit, not just before and after. The channel itself is a checkpoint.

8\. \*\*EVERYTHING ENTERS SOLID, EXITS FLUID\*\* (P.37): The terminal \`okol\` \= phase-shift to fluid. Distillation complete.

\#\# F75R ‚Üí F77V ‚Äî THE SIX-FOLIO SYSTEM

| \# | Folio | Function | Question | Status |  
|---|-------|----------|----------|--------|  
| 1 | f75r | Network Initialization | HOW does the system work? | DEFINED |  
| 2 | f75v | Scale-Up | HOW MUCH can it handle? | DEFINED |  
| 3 | f76r | Stability Specification | WHAT RULES govern it? | DEFINED |  
| 4 | f76v | Endurance Testing | HOW LONG can it run? | TESTED |  
| 5 | f77r | Routing Controller | WHERE does material flow? | MAPPED |  
| 6 | f77v | Full State Machine | COMPLETE LIFECYCLE | \*\*ASSEMBLED\*\* |

After six folios, the system is fully DEFINED, TESTED, MAPPED, and ASSEMBLED into a working machine. The remaining fourteen folios (f78r‚Äìf84v) apply this machine to specific purification tasks: dual-stream processing, fixed-point convergence, modular cells, maintenance protocols, distributed coordination, gentle handling, and more.

\# ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê  
\# FOLIO F78R ‚Äî DUAL-BATCH PROCESSING  
\# TWO CHARGES THROUGH SHARED INFRASTRUCTURE  
\# ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê

\#\# 1\. COMPLETE IMAGE DESCRIPTION

Folio 78 recto presents a bath system showing TWO SEQUENTIAL STREAMS processed through the same network. Margin labels name physical routing elements. Reflux loops visible where output feeds back to input. The page is split into two halves by a \`p\!\!\!\` header at P.26 and a \`=\` boundary at P.25, representing two separate charges (batches) run through IDENTICAL infrastructure.

\*\*What distinguishes this page:\*\* REUSABLE PROCESSING. Where f77v showed a complete single-batch state machine, f78r shows that same infrastructure processing TWO BATCHES IN SEQUENCE. The equipment is NOT cleaned between batches ‚Äî residual material from Batch 1 PRIMES the infrastructure for Batch 2\. This is CONTINUOUS PRODUCTION.

\*\*Visual layout:\*\* Three channel keys (X.3, X.4, X.5) label physical tubes in the margins. Batch 1 occupies P.1‚ÄìP.25 (25 paragraphs). Batch 2 occupies P.26‚ÄìP.41 (16 paragraphs). The asymmetry is deliberate: Batch 1 does more PRODUCTION work, Batch 2 does more VERIFICATION work.

\*\*What a fifteenth-century practitioner saw:\*\* The PRODUCTION SCHEDULE. Run one charge through the distillation train, seal it, then immediately load the second charge into the same vessels ‚Äî still warm, still primed with residual flux. The second charge starts faster because the equipment remembers the first.

\*\*What a fifteenth-century patient saw:\*\* The MORNING AND AFTERNOON BATH REGIMEN. First group enters in the morning (Batch 1), proceeds through the full circuit, exits purified. Second group enters in the afternoon (Batch 2\) into water already heated and mineralized by the first group's passage.
